class="ci-player-bio-content"><p>Nicknamed "Hurricane" for his ability to change games in no time, the big-hitting Deepak Hooda was one of India's go-to men during his Under-19s tenure in 2014. In the same year, Hooda became the second Baroda player after Snehal Parikh to score a century on first-class debut. But it was during his debut IPL season for Rajasthan Royals, in 2015, that Hooda's powerful striking abilities were more widely taken note of - he scored 151 runs in 14 matches at a strike-rate of 158.94.
